				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20271564' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 960;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

						<div id="earlyAccessHeader" class="early_access_header">
							<div class="heading">
																	<h1 class="inset">抢先体验游戏</h1>
									<h2 class="inset">立刻获取体验权限然后开始游戏，并随着游戏的发展参与其中。</h2>
									<p><span>注意：</span>该抢先体验的游戏内容尚不完整且也许会发生变化。如果您目前不是特别想玩这款游戏，那么您应该等待一段时间来观察游戏的开发进度。<a href="https://store.steampowered.com/earlyaccessfaq/?snr=1_5_9_">了解更多</a></p>
															</div>
							<div id="earlyAccessBody" class="devnotes">
																	<div class="devs_say">开发者的话：</div>
								
								<div id="devnotes_expander">
																			<h1>为何要采用抢先体验这种模式？</h1>
										“Throughout the development of Legendary Tales we have always worked closely with players and the gaming community to make our game the best it can be. Now we are coming to steam to continue that work. We want to gather more community feedback and have players be a part of the final part of our development process.”

										<h1>这款游戏的抢先体验状态大约持续多久？</h1>
										“We are aiming to launch the full game around the early 2023 but it could be earlier if the early access release goes well.”

										<h1>计划中的完整版本和抢先体验版本到底有多少不同？</h1>
										“We plan to add more content to the game. The most important additions include more monsters, more weapon types and more <br>
items (Especially more legendary items). We are also planning to add more dungeon themes to provide a wider variety of maps. <br>
The added monsters will also include champion monsters and boss fights.”

										<h1>抢先体验版本的现状如何？</h1>
										“The current version of Legendary tales includes most of the gameplay as it will appear in the final game, outside of any bug fixes; gameplay and mechanics are mostly completed. <br><br><strong>Currently available/working features include:</strong><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li> Physics based combat<br></li><li> Pre-designed dungeon system**<br></li><li> Dungeon quests**<br></li><li> Player attribute system (Still working on balance)<br></li><li> Tutorial level<br></li><li> Homebase town with working shops<br></li><li> Game of chance mechanic in town blackmarket<br></li><li> Random number generated items**<br></li><li> Legendary items with each unique combat skills**<br></li><li> Magics **<br></li><li>Skill tree system</li></ul> ** Limited variations compared to full release.<br><br>We wanted to release into early access a version of the game that would give players a true feel for how the final version will turn out. That way we can focus on adding more content and making minor tweaks to bring a truly fantastic experience to VR.”

										<h1>在抢先体验期间和结束之后，游戏价格会有所不同吗？</h1>
										“Yes, the early access version will be cheaper than the full release due to the amount of content that will be added to the completed game.”

										<h1>在开发过程中，你们是如何计划让玩家社区参与进来的？</h1>
										“We've been working with the community since early on in the development of Legendary Tales, it's been a rollercoaster of a ride, but our interactions with players have truly helped to shape the game into what it is now. Now that we are moving on to this next stage we want to continue our community engagement. We have a clear vision for what we want Legendary Tales to be and we want to use the community feedback to make it the best possible version of that. We want to work with players to improve game balance, fix any bugs and gather new ideas for items.”

																	</div> <!-- /devnotes_expander -->
								<a class="morebutton" id="devnotes_more" href="#" onclick="$J('#devnotes_expander').css({'max-height': 'none'}); $J(this).hide(); return false;">了解更多</a>
							</div>
						</div>

It\u2019s been a really long time since we\u2019ve had an update for you. Legendary Tales is a project that has been mired by a ridiculous amount of engine related troubles in its time. Those of you who have been with us a long while know this isn\u2019t the first time it\u2019s happened, but we had to switch our project, once again, to another engine version.\n\n\n[h2][b]Engine Changed : UE5 -> UE4 [\/b][\/h2]\n\nUnreal Engine 5 looked very promising, and we were very excited to use it, however, despite all our best efforts at optimizing Chaos physics engine there were still going to be players who would have ended up left behind. We were able to save 25% of the CPU cost, but it was still 35% higher than UE4 in multi-play, which would have meant many of our fans would have had performance problems.\n\nWe really felt it wasn\u2019t worth abandoning the majority of our players for this (Obviously) so we had to move back to Unreal Engine 4. This ended up sucking up at least 3-5 months. \nDuring last year\u2019s announcement I had mentioned that this was a potential risk, and unfortunately it didn't end the way we had hoped. We're really sorry that things ended up this way, but we're back and situated in UE4 now. \n\nThere is a possibility to upgrade the engine sometime in the future after release, but we don't want to waste any more time on trying to make it happen now, especially when our fans have been so patient already.\n\nWe also wanted to let you know, despite us not appearing very active on Steam we have been seeing things. We know a lot of people think the game is dead, that's understandable. We can all think of a game where we got burned by developers just abandoning their ideas. \n\nBut I want to assure you it\u2019s not dead, our lack of communication is partly because we were spending so much time and energy on moving engines and due to some health issues. \n\nI know some of you are aware I had been needing to go to the hospital for a while, well I finally did, and I ended up having to stay and recover for a lot longer than anticipated, while work continued here at the office it was harder to communicate with you and the team. \n\nWe can\u2019t promise that the next few months will include a lot of communication, but we hope you can believe us that the game is not dead, and development is absolutely ongoing. \n\nSo, because of all of this we were not able to release or update earlier this year, however the next update will in fact be the full release. Legendary Tales 1.0.\n\nAlso, to inform you, there will be no early access test this time as we have been doing closed Beta tests for quite a while now. 							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/NextGenerationARPG.png?t=1657877387"><br>Collect loot, explore dungeons, take down enemies and grow your own unique character build. Do all this alone or together with friends in this one of a kind VR experience. <br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/RPGAttributeSystem.png?t=1657877387"><br>Build your own character through natural gameplay and traditional ARPG character creation.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/Multiplayer.png?t=1657877387"><br>Up to 4 player co-op<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/SkillTree.png?t=1657877387"><br>Advance your character by making your way through an extensive skill tree. <br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/Magic.png?t=1657877387"><br>Learn magic spells and destroy your enemies with fire, ice or lightning spells.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/CollectibleRNGItem.png?t=1657877387"><br>Collect an almost limitless amount of items thanks to random number generation.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/Physics.png?t=1657877387"><br>Physics based fighting system with destructible items<br><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_01_Comp.gif?t=1657877387"><br>Are you ready to step down into the darkness? Explore predesigned dungeons alone or with friends, but be careful, there are monsters waiting down there for you. Luckily, you have a myriad of ways to fight back. Bash them with bludgeoning tools, Slice them with swords, Ambush them with archery and daggers or use magic to hit them with a hex.<br>With physics-based melee combat, improved AI, Random number generated items, up to 4 player co-op and an RPG style attribute system, those with a yearning for adventure in a fantasy RPG setting are sure to find everything they need right here.<br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_02.gif?t=1657877387"><br><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_VR.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">Built from the ground up for VR, Legendary Tales has great optimisation for any PCVR platform and customisable graphics settings to ensure you get the best possible experience.</ul><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_Multiplayer.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">Up to 4 player multiplayer is permitted in Legendary Tales, grab some friends, trade items, and take on a dungeon together, all in VR!</ul><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_Physics.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">Legendary tales has a masterful physics-based fighting system made to mimic the feeling of really using weapons while still keeping it fun to play. Weapons have a weight that determines how easy they are to swing, swing with more force to do more damage. It's not just the weapons where we've improved the physics though, enemy feedback and interactive objects also react according to how hard you hit them. </ul><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_Items.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">The items in Legendary Tales provide a huge amount of different fighting styles to try out. Don't try to catch them all though, random number generated items means there's an insane amount of item so there's plenty of variety for you to choose from. Items are also graded from normal to legendary, with legendary being the rarest, the best and of course, the coolest. </ul><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_CombatSkills.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">The items in Legendary Tales also have their own combat skills to really spice up your take downs. Slashing items allow you to dismember enemies, bludgeoning items will let you stun them and legendary items have their own unique skills for you to discover. Use multiple items together to use their combat skill in conjunction. Find the right combination of weapon, armor and helmet FOR YOU to build your best system.</ul><br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1465070/extras/LT_About_Attributes.png?t=1657877387"><br><ul class="bb_ul">Also included is an RPG style attribute system that grows naturally with your game play. As well as other perks that you will have to learn as you play. Increase your damage by increasing your strength, make less noise when moving by increasing your dexterity, or just increase your chances of better item drops by increasing your luck! Grow your character in your way! Character attributes are Strength, Dexterity, Vitality, Intellect, Wisdom, Luck  </ul> <br><br><br>You can experience all of this in VR! So put on your headset and head into the dungeon to start creating your own Legendary Tales.						</div>

									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Legendary Tales 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary140595462_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：6 月 24 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>

				<div class="content">
					I feel like this is something that I need to address because people are getting over their heads about, and it kinda gives me mixed emotions.<br><br>Probably below these reviews you're gonna see "Abandoned game, dead game" and its easy to say that at face value. Sure they promised a massive update at the end of last year, but let me tell you why it did not happen. But first let me address a lot of peoples issues<br><br>"Theres no update" or "Devs are keeping quiet"<br>First of all this is a lie. You can reach out to the devs on the discord, and most of the time they respond. They even have pinned comments on #general if you want to see whats happened.<br>          Right now the main developer has undergone surgery, and there is someone beta testing the game. That was of two <br>          weeks ago, the main Developer is still recovering. <br><br>Devs aren't quiet, in fact they tell you why. They state its a unreal 5 engine. This game was made in 4, so importing in the new engine has caused problems. Sure they might not say what specifically but I think its easy to decode what.<br><br>Usually models don't just "disappear" and usually importing them isn't the main problem. I think the main issue is coding. Programming takes a lot, and I would not be surprised if they had to recode more than they expected. It would also explain why they don't say what specifically, because if I was a DEV and said "The engine is stating invalid class/variables within the class" I dont think a lot of people would understand that. Im a basic ass programmer, and I probably did not even make up an error correctly, that being said I think that doubles the argument.<br><br><br>TL:DR please stop saying dead game, when the devs are very much alive.<br><br><br>***Edit***<br><br>They came out with an update on the scenario they're in, now stop complaining					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 3.4 小时												（评测时 3.4 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Legendary Tales 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary140345832_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：6 月 20 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					The recent mixed reviews for this game are a joke, this game is phenomenal. If you are looking to buy this game, look no further. This game is one of the best VR dungeon crawlers you can buy right now. This game has great combat, and it doesn't make you feel like a outrageous god on a blood lust like blade and sorcery does, but it makes the combat more satisfying, and rewarding. When your fighting, you actually need to block and parry attacks instead of rushing and pushing over people like you would in blade and sorcery, the fighting is something you should actually practice in Legendary Tales, and the combat feels more fun because of it.<br><br> There are downsides, as well. Like the repetitive enemies (Skeletons, Bats, and Goblins) but its not all bad because there are different variants, sizes, health of some different ones, but sometimes the buff enemies are another downside. Sometimes you will come across "mini bosses" that are just big skeletons or goblins, they are really strong and I find myself dying to them way too much, and being spawned back into the village for the fourth time after dying from the boss while just trying to grab your dropped stuff is the most annoying thing in this game. That's the only complaints about combat I have, which annoyances should hopefully be fixed in the next update I hope. The rest of the game is great, and there is a lot to come for this game.<br><br>For the people who think this game was abandoned by the developers, the discord server's community is relatively active and you can find a little bit of information about the infamous and delayed update. The developers have not said much about progress about the update, nor a release date. Yet they say in the discord that the game is being worked on avidly, even if they do not say anything about it.					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 3.9 小时												（评测时 1.9 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Legendary Tales 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary142344514_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：7 月 19 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					with the content the game currently has, which while decent isn't ginormous or anything, i dont think its quite worth the current pricetag unless you're really itching for a game like this.<br><br>the melee combat is very fun, enemies and their attacks are all slightly 'limp physics' as opposed to the more 'rigid' style that B&amp;S has for example...this makes hitting enemies feel a bit better in some ways as they get moved a bit more with swings, plus the game has an impaling system that even lets you pull the weapons out sideways by 'cutting through' them, though afaik it doesnt do more damage, just feels good to do. its certainly a different feel to the flow of combat compared ot B&amp;S, where with that game attacks feel a bit stiff and a bit too 'canned' or over the top sometimes. here everything feels like it leans more into the physics side of it, and generally feels better imo.<br><br>personally some of the spell effects are lackluster, im talking how they look/feel...though most of what ive tried is some fire and the first lightning spell, it's basically a taser but you can shoot it, and i like my magic feeling powerful/looking good so that kinda dissapoints me, hopefully they can be improved sometime down the line to look a bit nicer (or maybe the first spells just look lackluster on purpose). the portal spell looks really nice though.<br><br>a new update looks like its on the horizon that should add a good # of things, incl more spells!<br><br>the way weapons handle feels good, 2 handers work nicely, feels good to try and parry and counter enemies, i find myself roleplaying a bit with it instead of trying to be efficient and get a ton of hits in when i parry or just punching enemies to death (punching is a little OP atm).<br><br>goblins are funny, they run away and often slam into walls comically.<br><br>either grab the game if you love VR physics based melee combat, or if you're on the fence, wait till it's on sale for 20something or less, i think. great game imo					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="content">
					Mondjuk azt hogy rossz és jó.. Sajnos az első videó ami az áruházi oldalon fel van tűntetve az nem a játék vagyis nem az amivel én játszottam . Ez 2023.08.14 én volt amikor még a  beígért update ami az első videón szerepel nem volt a játékban . Sajnos refund lett a vége, egy óra repetatív kaszabolás után. Nekem sajnos nagyon üres még az egész a crafting hiányzik nagyon . Viszont a concept nagyon jó ha tartják magukat a fejlesztők ahoz amit ígérnek . Nem mondom azt , hogy amikor az update megtörténik nem nézek rá vissza . De addig számomra csalódás volt picit . Aki azon gondolkodik hogy megvegye én azt ajánlom személy szerint várjatok vele, lehet nem kell sokat de lehet hogy ellégé megváratnak minket . Viszont ha bekerül amit ígérnek teljes mértékben megéri !					<div class="gradient"></div>

									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Legendary Tales 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary101064765_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2021 年 10 月 15 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					中秋节，又称祭月节、月光诞、月夕、秋节、仲秋节、拜月节、月娘节、月亮节、团圆节等，是中国民间的传统节日。中秋节源自天象崇拜，由上古时代秋夕祭月演变而来。中秋节自古便有祭月、赏月、吃月饼、玩花灯、赏桂花、饮桂花酒等民俗，流传至今，经久不息。<br>中秋节起源于上古时代，普及于汉代，定型于唐朝初年，盛行于宋朝以后。中秋节是秋季时令习俗的综合，其所包含的节俗因素，大都有古老的渊源。中秋节以月之圆兆人之团圆，为寄托思念故乡，思念亲人之情，祈盼丰收、幸福，成为丰富多彩、弥足珍贵的文化遗产。 <br>最初“祭月节”的节期是在干支历二十四节气“秋分”这天，后来才调至夏历八月十五日。 [46]  中秋节与春节、清明节、端午节并称为中国四大传统节日。受中华文化的影响，中秋节也是东亚和东南亚一些国家尤其是当地的华人华侨的传统节日。  2006年5月20日，国务院将其列入首批国家级非物质文化遗产名录。自2008年起中秋节被列为国家法定节假日。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="posted">

				<div class="persona_name"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198328688473/" data-miniprofile="368422745">bulldozer139</a></div>
												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198328688473/recommended/">20 篇评测</a></div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary99207489_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561198328688473/recommended/1465070/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 139.9 小时												（评测时 4.0 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Legendary Tales 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary99207489_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2021 年 9 月 12 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					玩了114小时了，目前总结下感受：<br>优点：<br>击剑拦截格挡效果不错。<br>怪物动画流畅。<br>随机地图很好。<br>总BOSS憨憨可爱(屁)。<br>传奇武器爆率增加后，很爽！<br><br>缺点：<br>怪物种类太单一，攻击方式单一，习惯后毫无挑战性....(除了狂暴加速BOSS外)<br>可以快速跑通关(只要不遇上减速BOSS，S型走位躲开弓箭手，拉火车通关不是梦)。<br>之前以为是移动速度BUG的目前发现，原来有个步行和跑步切换功能....但目前来看走路没必要....纯属添乱....<br>属性升级方式不自由，属性提升靠使用特定攻击或挨打提升，误提升了没用属性后无法反悔。且更新后武器攻击力提升巨大，导致属性的作用被进一步削弱...除了智力。<br>目前具备嘲讽功能的只有一个传奇盾牌......想练坦克很麻烦....<br>困难通关模式后无所事事.....总BOSS打死后没有宝箱奖励.....<br>宣传和教程中的 双手合并 魔法无法使用，只能使用单手魔法！<br>宣传视频里 举起罐子砸怪操作 实际上没有伤害。只能砸晕一会儿怪物....<br>魔法每次使用都需要打开一次菜单选择一次魔法.....哪怕重复使用同一种魔法......<br>无法潜行暗杀，敏捷降低移动脚步声没卵用....教程里的匕首暗杀毫无意义.....<br>目前已知某个传奇装备和某种属性搭配时会有 无敌 效果，人物不会死亡，哪怕最终BOSS都打不死你！:)<br>加智力的法师是这个 游戏最厉害的角色，而不是战士。。。尤其拿到某些OB的传奇武器的法师....因为不缺MP...传奇武器伤害又与属性关系不大....<br><br>总体来说，值得推荐。不错的游戏，虽然价格很贵(与目前质量相比)，而且后期会很无聊，尤其拿到部分OB的传奇武器.....虽然很爽....但那种单人或多人一起冒险，紧张刺激的合力打半天，互相配合打死怪的感觉荡然无存了。<br>传奇武器的爆率提升了，确实玩起来舒服了，但是某些传奇武器真的应该平衡下，否则冒险游戏就变成了秒怪游戏了.....传奇武器提升了乐趣，但其中一些OB的传奇武器又让这种提升变得素然无味.....<br>最后，目前游戏的打击感依然只有怪物挥剑时通过对等挥剑拦截格挡这一点。对于身体冲撞，盾击，被击中等情况，怪物依然没有任何物理性反馈....<br><br>I have played for 114 hours, and now I summarize my feelings:<br>advantage:<br>The fencing interception block works well.<br>The monster animation is smooth.<br>The random map is good (the whole map is random).<br>The total boss is simple and cute (fart).<br>After the explosion rate of legendary weapons has increased, it's cool!<br><br>shortcoming:<br>The monster type is too single, the attack method is single, and it is not challenging after getting used to it... (except for the violent acceleration BOSS)<br>You can quickly run through the level (as long as you don't encounter the slowing boss, the S-shaped walk avoids the archer, and it is not a dream to pull the train to clear the level).<br>I thought it was a movement speed bug. I found out that there was a switch function between walking and running.... But at the moment, walking is unnecessary.... It's pure chaos....<br>The method of attribute upgrade is not free. The attribute upgrade depends on the use of specific attacks or beatings. If you upgrade the useless attributes by mistake, you cannot go back. And after the update, the weapon's attack power has increased tremendously, resulting in further weakening of the role of attributes...except for intellect.<br>At present, there is only one legendary shield with taunt function...It is very troublesome to train tank...<br>There is nothing to do after the hard mode.....There is no treasure chest reward after the boss is killed.....<br>The combination of two hands magic in the promotion and tutorial cannot be used, only one-handed magic can be used!<br>In the promotional video, the operation of raising the can and smashing the monsters did not actually hurt. Only stun the monster for a while...<br>Every time you use magic, you need to open the menu and select magic once...even if you use the same magic repeatedly...<br>Can't stealthily assassinate, it's useless to reduce the sound of moving footsteps quickly....The dagger assassination in the tutorial is meaningless...<br>At present, it is known that a certain legendary equipment will have an invincible effect when matched with a certain attribute, and the character will not die, even if the boss cannot kill you in the end! :)<br>The wizard with Intellect is the most powerful character in this game, not a strength fighter. . . Especially the mage who got some OB legendary weapons...Because there is no shortage of MP...Legendary weapon damage has little to do with attributes...<br><br>Overall, it is recommended. Good game, although the price is very expensive (compared to the current quality), and the later stage will be very boring, especially to get some of the legendary weapons of OB.....Although it is very cool...but the kind of single or multiplayer Taking risks together, fighting together for a long time with intense excitement, the feeling of cooperating with each other to kill the monsters disappeared.<br>The explosion rate of legendary weapons has increased, and it is really comfortable to play, but some legendary weapons should really be balanced, otherwise the adventure game will become a second-guess game... Legendary weapons have increased the fun, but some of them OB's legendary weapon makes this improvement completely tasteless...<br>Finally, the current game's sense of percussion is still the only thing that monsters can use to intercept and block when they swing their swords peer-to-peer. For physical collisions, shield attacks, and being hit, the monster still does not have any physical feedback...<br>Oh, yes, the painful thorns + heavy rain + freezing technique are released at the same time, and the extension game may crash when online!					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="content">
					优秀物理互动与传统RPG的完美融合其结果导致我3天肝了24小时，这游戏令人着魔！<br>画面：我给90分<br>虚幻4引擎带来了优秀的画面效果与写实的物理互动，为了最大程度保证流畅度，这款VR游戏竟然同时支持DLSS和FSR，在双重优化下保证VR入门级显卡都能流畅游戏，中高端显卡更是因此获得近乎完美的VR体验！<br><br>游戏性：我给99分<br>你玩过最优秀的中世纪格斗VR是哪款？剑与魔法？如果我说这游戏还原了其物理效果的90%你是否会提起一丝兴趣？如果再加入暗黑破坏神的装备系统你是否已经开始想要体验一下了？别急，这游戏不仅复刻了暗黑，甚至还借鉴了黑魂，并且地图每次都是随机生成，而且这一切还建立在最多4人联机的基础上，如果你沉迷于刷刷刷的快感，又想要秀一把人品拿新鲜出炉的史诗级装备在队友面前装逼，这游戏绝对适合你！<br><br>优点<br>画面优秀<br>全物理碰撞<br>种类繁多的装备<br>随机不重样的地图<br>联机体验非常优秀<br>无需加速器<br><br>缺点<br>贵，真的死贵<br><br>					<div class="gradient"></div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary128042254_leftcol_ctn"></div>

				<div class="content">
					整体体验还可以，最好有同伴一起联机，体验还是不错的。<br>p2p联机，如果连不上或者延迟高的话推荐使用p2p party之类的p2p联机工具。<br>缺点就是重复游玩性略差，虽然是随机生成地图，但本质也只是相同地形的房间进行排列组合，多打几关之后就会经常感觉，这个房间地形怎么这么眼熟。<br>另外流程也比较短，和朋友双人联机，10小时出头就见到boss了，因为没怎么刷等级装备，所以惨败_(:_」∠)_不过如果打完了boss，那也就直接通关了，没什么其他游玩空间，相对于这个价位来说感觉不太值。<br>作者6月份画大饼，承诺年内会更新更大的出生村子，更多种类的地牢，更随机的地图，更多的武器，更多的敌人，更多的动作，但是眼看这都12月了，也没什么进展……不知道什么时候能出来					<div class="gradient"></div>
